File E:\BG3_Unpack\Gustav_pak\Mods\GustavDev\Story\Dialogs\Act3\LowerCity\HouseOfHope\LOW_HouseOfHope_Archivist.lsj
Synopsis:
Dialogue with Archivist in House of Hope. He is the person who keep records on all Raphael projects. Half-way between a curator and an accountant, he's incredibly repressed, and obsessed with record-keeping and accounts. He's the model of Order and tidiness, but being from the hells, he's also hiding a dark secret. In his case, he's a masochist, and finds the concept of breaking rules thrilling, though he hates to admit it. Strict and severe, he will try to keep order unless the player leans on his vices or fears, in which case he'll become flustered and dismiss them to the boudoir.

File E:\BG3_Unpack\Gustav_pak\Mods\GustavDev\Story\Dialogs\Act3\LowerCity\HouseOfHope\LOW_HouseOfHope_HopeSpirit01.lsj
Synopsis:
First dialogue with Hope's spirit that happens after players get to House of Hope. Hope is a captive within the House, and has been driven mad by years of psychological and physical torture. Raphael keeps her alive because she astonishes him - and the reason for that is that no matter what he does to her, she holds onto the last of her hope and optimism. That fascinates him. In this dialogue, Hope introduces players to the House of Hope. They have arrived here deliberately, knowing that they are not invited, and that it is likely dangerous. Hope appears to warn them of that danger, and to help them, and also introduces the deranged vibe of the area. Note: When Hope speaks in all-caps, she is showing the manic side of her personality. Louder, more intense, and almost like she's possessed by a different, more deranged version of herself.

File E:\BG3_Unpack\Gustav_pak\Mods\GustavDev\Story\Dialogs\Act3\LowerCity\HouseOfHope\LOW_HouseOfHope_PAD_BoudoirDisguiseWarning.lsj
Synopsis:
Players get a disguise in House of Hope as an attire item: while it's equipped, Eternal Debtors are not hostile towards the character. In Boudoir there's a big chance that one character will be naked (after all the items are unequipped) after an encounter with Incubus, so we place a small warning near the exit if a character is not in disguise
